#c 3393206 2019-11-12 17:42:23
[Bob] import turtle
def triangle(x,n):
if n==0:
for angle in [0,120,120]:
turtle.lt(angle)
turtle.fd(x)
turtle.lt(120)
else:
triangle(x/2,n-1)
turtle.forward(x/2)
triangle(x/2,n-1)
turtle.lt(120)
turtle.forward(x / 2)
turtle.right(120)
triangle(x/2,n-1)
turtle.right(120)
turtle.forward(x/2)
turtle.lt(120)
n=int(input())
turtle.setup(800,800)
turtle.speed(0)
turtle.penup()
turtle.goto(-200,-200)
turtle.pendown()
turtle.pensize(2)
triangle(400,n)
turtle.done()
